   <!-- /Component - slideshow -->
   <script id="component-slideshow">
    /* /inc/component-slideshow.php *//*2018-03-29 17:43:49*/  

		$(document).ready(function(){

			if($("body").hasClass("home") && $(".autoplay").length == 0) $(".slideshow").eq(0).css("opacity", "1");

			$(".slideshow figure").first().addClass("cycle-slide-active");

			$('.loadImg').on("click", function(e) {
				e.stopImmediatePropagation();
				$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop:  $("h1").offset().top-280 }, 'fast');
				return false;
			});

			if ( ($("body").hasClass("product") || $("body").hasClass("where")) && $("h1").length > 0){
				$(".slideshow")
					.click(function(){
						$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop:  $(".nav-bar").offset().top-175}, 'slow');
					})
					.one('cycle-after', function(){$(this).find(".main-header").removeClass("visible")})
					.append("<div class='main-header visible'><div>" +
						"<h1>" + $("h1").first().text() + "</h1>" +
						"<h2>" + $("h1").next("h2").text() + "</h2>" +
						"</div></div>");
				var nightsPrice = $(".nights-price");
				UV.btnAvailability = $('.special-bt [onclick^="loadAvailability"]');
				if ( UV.product.price_indication !== null ) {
					$(nightsPrice).clone().appendTo(".main-header>div");
				}
				if ( $(".main-header").outerHeight() > 200 ) {
					$(".main-header>div").css({"max-width":"480px"});
				}

				if ( UV.page.type=="property" || UV.page.type=="itinerary" ) {
					if ( UV.product.price_indication !== null ) {
						$(".main-header .nights-price")
							.after( makeCta({
								label: UV.btnAvailability.length ? 'Show availability' : $(nightsPrice).data('btnwithprice'),
								link: ( UV.btnAvailability.length ? "javascript:$(UV.btnAvailability).trigger('click');void(0);" :
										( $('#enquiry_form').length ? "javascript:$('html,body').animate({scrollTop:$('#enquiry_form').offset().top-295},'slow');void(0)" : "javascript:contact_us();void(0);" )
									),
								click:"event.stopPropagation()"
							})
						).find( UV.btnAvailability.length ? 'li:first-child' : 'X' ).remove();
					} else {
						$(".main-header>div")
							.append(
								( UV.page.type=="property"
									? $(nightsPrice).data('message')
									: ''
								) +
								( $('[data-id="tab-Itineraries"] a').length
									? makeCta({label:$(nightsPrice).data('btnwithitin')})
									: makeCta({label:$(nightsPrice).data('btndefault'),link:"javascript:contact_us();void(0);"})
								)
							)
							.find('p, a').on('click', function(event){
								event.stopPropagation();
								if ( $('[data-id="tab-Itineraries"] a').length ) {
									$('html,body').animate({scrollTop:$("nav.product-tabs").offset().top-225},'slow');
									$('[data-id="tab-Itineraries"] a').trigger('click');
								}

							});
					}

				} else if ( UV.page.type=="region" || UV.page.type=="sub region" || UV.page.type=="country" || UV.page.type=="area" ) {

					$(".main-header>div")
						.append( makeCta({
							style: "margin:-1rem auto 2rem",
							label: "See " + ( readCookie("LTG_GeoData").indexOf("US|") == 0 ? 'trips' : 'holidays' ),
							link: "javascript:$('html,body').animate({scrollTop:$('.search-tabs').offset().top-354},'slow');void(0)",
							click:"event.stopPropagation()"
						})
					);

				}
				function makeCta(options) {
					return '<div class="special-bt"' +
						(options && options.style ? 'style="' + options.style + '" ' : '' ) +
						'><a class="bg-cta" ' +
						(options && options.click ? 'onclick="' + options.click + '" ' : '' ) +
						'href="' + (options && options.link ? options.link : 'javascript:void(0)' ) +	'">' +
						(options && options.label ? options.label : 'Make an enquiry' ) +
						'<span><svg><use xlink:href="#svg-arrow-stroke"/></svg></span></a></div>';
				}

			}



			var w = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth;

			$(".slideshow").each(function(){

				var wSlide = $(this).find(".loadImg img").first().attr("src").match(/width=(.*)/i);
				wSlide = (wSlide) ? parseInt(wSlide[1]) : 1920;

				if($(this).find(".cycle-slideshow").length > 0){

					var s = $(this);
					var gal = eval( $(this).find(".cycle-slideshow").attr("data-variable") );

					if($("body").hasClass("home") || $("body").hasClass("what")){
						var finalW = ((window.devicePixelRatio > 1 || w >= wSlide) ? wSlide : (w <= 1024) ? 1024 : (w <= 1366) ? 1366 : (w <= 1600) ? 1600 : 1920 );
					}else{
						var finalW = (( window.devicePixelRatio > 1 || w >= wSlide ) ? wSlide : (w < 1366) ? 1024 : (w < 1600) ? 1366 : (w < 1920) ? 1600 : 1920 );
					}



					$(gal.gallery_imgs).each(function(index, val){

						if(val['Caption'].substring(0,4)=="url:"){
							$(s).find("figure").eq(index).css({"cursor":"pointer"}).on("click",function(e){
								document.location=val['Caption'].substring(4);
							});
						}

						if(w > finalW){
							var currW = (index < 2) ? wSlide : finalW;
							$(s).find(".img").eq(index).wrap('<div class="blur-bg" style="background-image:url(\'' + slideURL + val['ImageId'] + '&width=' + currW + '\');" ></div>');
						}
						
						if(index > 1){
							$(s).find(".img").eq(index).css({"background-image" : "url('" + slideURL + val['ImageId'] + '&width=' + finalW + "')"});
						}
						
						$(s).find(".img").eq(index).css({"max-width" : finalW + "px"});

					});

				}

			});
			
		});
   </script>

   <script>
    $(document).ready(function(){
		
		/* make loadImg clickable for scroll down */
		$('.video h4').on("click touchstart", function(e) {
			e.stopImmediatePropagation();
			$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop:  $("h1").offset().top-280 }, 'fast');
			return false;
		});
		
		if($("body").hasClass("home") && $(".autoplay").length > 0){
			$(".cycle-slideshow").eq(0).cycle("pause");			
			$(".slideshow").eq(0).css({"position": "absolute", "z-index": "-1"});
			
			$.getScript( "https://player.vzaar.com/libs/flashtakt/client.js" )
				.done(function( script, textStatus ) {
					
				console.log( textStatus );
				
				var iframe = $(".videos iframe").eq(0);
				var v = $(iframe).attr("name");
				
				var vzp = new vzPlayer(v);

				vzp.ready(function() {
					
					console.log("video ready");
					
					//vzp.play2();
					$(iframe).animate({opacity:1}, 1000);
					//setTimeout(function(){$(iframe).parent().css("background-image", "");}, 1000);
					
					vzp.addEventListener("progress", function(v){
						console.log(v);
						if(v == "100percent"){
							switchToSlideshow();
						}
						
					});
				})
					
				})
				.fail(function( jqxhr, settings, exception ) {
					console.log("ERROR loading vzaar js");
					switchToSlideshow();
				});
		}
		
		function switchToSlideshow(){
			$(".videos").eq(0).animate({opacity:0}, 1000, function(){$(this).find("iframe").remove()});
			$(".slideshow").eq(0).css("z-index", "1").animate({opacity:1}, 1000, function(){
				console.log("complete");
				$(".cycle-slideshow").eq(0).cycle("resume");
			});
		}
		
		$(".videos > h4").click(function(){
			$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop:  $("h1").offset().top-280 }, 'fast');
		});

	});
   </script>
   <script id="component-media">
    /* 2018-01-19 10:52:25 Desktop media component */

	$(document).ready(function(){

		$(".media-wrap").not("div ~ .media-wrap, section ~ .media-wrap, form ~ .media-wrap").addClass("firstOne");

		var thumbsSpeed = 2000,
			thumbW	= 	55,
			defaultLeft = 45,
			show = 8,
			media = 1,
			players = [],
			youtubeApiLoaded = 0,
			arrdisplay = "visible";

		if($(".media .videos").hasClass("selected") && $(".media .videos iframe").attr("src").indexOf("youtube") > 0 ){
			youtubeScript();
		}

		$(".media-wrap").each(function(){
			$(this).attr("id", "media-"+media);
			$(this).find("input[name='media']").val(media);
			$(this).find(".videos iframe").attr("id", "video"+media);
			$(this).find(".map").attr("id", "map"+media);

			var thumbnailsW = show * thumbW + 90; // 90 - padding
			$(".media-wrap .thumbnails").css({width : thumbnailsW+'px', 'clip' :'rect(0,'+thumbnailsW+',30,0)'});

			var child = $(this).find(".slideshow");

			$(child).on("mouseout",function(){
				$(".carousel-content").removeClass("hover");
				$("#media-1 .slideshow .cycle-slideshow").cycle("resume");
			})

			if(child.length && $(child).find(".cycle-slideshow").length > 0){

				$(child).find('.cycle-slideshow').cycle('pause').parent().addClass("paused");

				var mediaWrap = $(this),
					gal = eval($(this).find(".cycle-slideshow").attr("data-variable")),
					w = $(window).width(),
					wSlide = $(this).find(".loadImg img").first().attr("src").match(/width=(.*)/i),
					wSlide = (wSlide) ? parseInt(wSlide[1]) : 1920;

				if ( $("body").hasClass("home") || $("body").hasClass("what") ) {
					var finalW = ((window.devicePixelRatio > 1 || w >= wSlide) ? wSlide : (w <= 1024) ? 1024 : (w <= 1366) ? 1366 : (w <= 1600) ? 1600 : 1920 );
				} else {
					var finalW = (( window.devicePixelRatio > 1 || w >= wSlide ) ? wSlide : ( w >= 1024 && w < 1366 ) ? 1024 : (w >= 1366 && w < 1600) ? 1366 : (w >= 1600 && w < 1920) ? 1600 : 1920 );
				}
				$(gal.gallery_imgs).each(function(index, val){
					$(mediaWrap).find(".thumbnails .slideshow-thumbs img").eq(index).attr('src',slideURL + val['ImageId'] + "&width=" + ((index <= 1) ? wSlide : finalW) );
				});

				firstInit("slideshow", $(child).hasClass("selected"));

				var thumbs = $("#media-"+media+" .slideshow-thumbs img").length;
				if ( show < thumbs ) {
					$(child).on('cycle-after', function( event, opts ) {
						var t = $(this).parent().find(".thumbnails");
						thumbsSlide(t.selector);
					});
				}

				$(child).on( 'cycle-pager-activated', function( event, opts ) {
					$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0}, 'fast');
					$("#media-1 .slideshow .cycle-slideshow").cycle("pause");
					$("#media-1 .slideshow figure").eq(opts.currSlide+1).find('.carousel-content').addClass("hover");
				});

				slideshowActive(media);
			}

			child = $(this).find(".videos");
			if ( child.length ) {
				firstInit("videos", $(child).hasClass("selected"));
			}

			if ( $(this).find(".map").length ){
				checkMap(media);
			}

			media++;

		});

		$('#media-1 .nav-bar').append('<div class="bt scroll"><div><svg><use xlink:href="#svg-arrow-stroke"/></svg></div></div>');

		$(".media-wrap .nav-bar").on("click touchstart", function(e) {
			$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0}, 'fast');
		});

		$(".media-wrap .bt").on("click touchstart", function(e) {

			if ( $(this).hasClass("scroll") ) {
				$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop:  $('h1[itemprop="name"]').offset().top-280 }, 'fast');
				e.stopPropagation();
				return false;
			}

			var m = $(this).parent().parent().find("input[name='media']").val(),
				go = $(this).attr("data-for");

			if ( !$("#media-"+m+" ."+go).hasClass("selected") ) {

				if($("html").hasClass("touch")){
					var cycle = $("#media-"+m+" .slideshow .cycle-slideshow");
					if(go != "slideshow"){
						$(cycle).cycle('pause');
					}else{
						$(cycle).cycle('resume');
					}
				}

				if(go == "videos" && youtubeApiLoaded == 0 ){
					youtubeScript();
				}

				$("#media-"+m).find(".media > div").removeClass("selected");
				$("#media-"+m+" ."+go).addClass("selected");

				$("#media-"+m+" .thumbs-holder").removeClass("selected");
				$("#media-"+m+" ."+go+"-thumbs").addClass("selected");

				$("#media-"+m+" .bt").removeClass("active");
				$(this).addClass("active");

				var thumbs = $("#media-"+m+" ."+go+"-thumbs img").length;
				visibilityArrow(m, thumbs);

				slideshowActive(m);
				stopVideo(m);
				checkMap(m);

			}

		});

		function firstInit(type, sel){
			var elem = $("#media-"+media+" ."+type+"-thumbs"),
				thumbs = $(elem).find("img").length,
				imgThumbsW = thumbs * thumbW,
				left = (show < thumbs) ? '45px' : 'calc((100% - '+imgThumbsW+'px )/2)';

			$(elem).css({width : imgThumbsW + 'px', "left" : left});

			$(elem).find("> *").eq(show-1).attr("id", "curr");

			if ( sel ) {
				$(elem).addClass("selected");
				visibilityArrow(media, thumbs);

				$("#media-"+media+" .bt[data-for='"+type+"']").addClass("active");
			}
		}

		function checkMap(m){
			if($("#map"+m).hasClass("selected") && $("#map"+m+" > *").length == 0){
				loadMap("map"+m, "initMap");
			}
		}


		function slideshowActive(m){

			if ( $("html").hasClass("touch") ) {
				return false;
			}

			var cycle = $("#media-" + m + " .slideshow .cycle-slideshow"),
				elem = $("#media-" + m + " .thumbnails, #media-"+m+" .buttons");

			if ( UV.page.type=="property" || UV.page.type=="itinerary" && $("#media-" + m + " .slideshow").hasClass("paused") ){

				setTimeout(function(){
					$("#media-" + m + " .slideshow").removeClass("paused");
					$(cycle).cycle('resume');
				},5000);

			} else {

				if($("#media-" + m + " .slideshow").hasClass("selected")){

					$(cycle).cycle('resume');

					$(elem).bind('mouseenter',function(){
						$(cycle).cycle('pause');
					});
					$(elem).bind('mouseleave', function(){
						$(cycle).cycle('resume');
					});

				} else {

					$(cycle).cycle('pause');
					$(elem).unbind("mouseenter mouseleave");

				}

			}

		}

		$(".media-wrap .videos-thumbs div").click(function(){

			var m = $(this).parent().parent().find("input[name='media']").val(),
				img = $(this).find("img");

			if(youtubeApiLoaded == 0 && $(img).attr("data-type").toLowerCase() == "youtube"){
				youtubeScript();
			}

			var videoId = $(img).attr("data-video"),
				videoLink = ($(img).attr("data-type").toLowerCase() == "vimeo") ? vimeoURL : youtubeURL;

			if($("body").hasClass("video-page")){
				videoLink += "&autoplay=1&rel=0";
			}

			var title = $(img).attr("data-title");
			videoLink = videoLink.replace("[placeholderID]", videoId);

			$("#media-"+m+" iframe").attr("src", videoLink);
			$("#media-"+m+" .video").css("background-image", "url('"+$(img).attr("src")+"')");
			$("#media-"+m+" .video h4").text(title);

			$("#media-"+m+" .videos-thumbs > div").removeClass("cycle-pager-active");
			$(this).addClass("cycle-pager-active");

		});
		function stopVideo(m) {

			if(youtubeApiLoaded == 0){
				return false;
			}

			if($("#media-"+m).find(".videos").length){
				var sel = $("#media-"+m+" .videos-thumbs .cycle-pager-active img").attr("data-type");
				if(sel == "vimeo"){
					vimeoVideo('pause', m);
				}else{
					players[m].pauseVideo();
				}
			}
		}
		function vimeoVideo(action, m){
			var iFram = document.getElementById('video'+m);
			var url = iFram.src.split('?')[0];
			var data = { method: action };

			if(url !== undefined){
				iFram.contentWindow.postMessage(JSON.stringify(data), url);
			}
		}

		function thumbsSlide(clicked, type){
			var index = $(clicked).parent().find("input[name='media']").val(),
				m = $("#media-"+index),
				thumbs = $(m).find(".thumbs-holder.selected img").length,
				currThumb = $(m).find(".thumbs-holder.selected #curr").index() + 1;

			if(!type ){

				var cycleCurr = $(m).find(".thumbs-holder.selected .cycle-pager-active").index()+1;

				if(cycleCurr <= (currThumb-show)){
					currThumb = (cycleCurr > show) ? cycleCurr : show;
				}else if(cycleCurr > currThumb){
					currThumb=cycleCurr;
				}else{
					return false;
				}

			}

			if(type == "next" && currThumb != thumbs){
				currThumb++;
			}
			if(type == "prev" && currThumb != show ){
				currThumb--;
			}

			var left = -(currThumb - show)*thumbW + defaultLeft;

			$("#media-"+index+" .thumbs-holder.selected").css({"left": left+'px'}).find("img").removeAttr("id");
			$("#media-"+index+" .thumbs-holder.selected img").eq(currThumb-1).attr("id", "curr");

			disabledArrow(currThumb, thumbs, index);

		}

		$(".media-wrap .next").click(function(){ thumbsSlide($(this).parent(), 'next');	});
		$(".media-wrap .prev").click(function(){ thumbsSlide($(this).parent(), "prev"); });

		function disabledArrow(currThumb, thumbs, media){
			var m = $("#media-"+media);
			if(currThumb == thumbs){
				$(m).find(".next").addClass("disabled");
			}else{
				$(m).find(".next").removeClass("disabled");
			}
			if(currThumb == show){
				$(m).find(".prev").addClass("disabled");
			}else{
				$(m).find(".prev").removeClass("disabled");
			}

		}

		function visibilityArrow(m, thumbs){
			arrdisplay = (show >= thumbs) ? 'hidden' : 'visible';
			$("#media-"+m).find(".prev, .next").css('visibility', arrdisplay);
		}

		function youtubeScript(){
			var tag = document.createElement('script');
			tag.src = "https://www.youtube.com/player_api";
			var firstScriptTag = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
			firstScriptTag.parentNode.insertBefore(tag, firstScriptTag);

			window.onYouTubePlayerAPIReady = function() {
				$(".videos").each(function(){
					youtubeApiLoaded = 1;
					var id = $(this).find("iframe").attr('id');
					if(id && $(this).find("iframe").attr('src').indexOf("youtube") > 0){
						players[ parseInt( id.replace(/[^\d.]/g, '') ) ] = new YT.Player(id);
					}
				});
			}

		}

	});
   </script>

    var subscribeURL = "/";
		
		$(document).ready(function(){
			$('#subscribe').on('submit',function(e) {

				$(this).find("fieldset").css("visibility", "hidden");
				loading("rgba(255,255,255,0.5)", "#subscribe");

				/* Do AJAX 'post' */
				var frm = $(this);
				$.ajax({
					type: "POST",
					url: subscribeURL,
					data: $(frm).serialize(),
					success: function(data) {
						closeLoading();
						$(frm).html(data.Message);
					}
				});
				return false;

			});
		})

          <script id="keyWordSearchBoxComponent">
           var savedSearches = localStorage.getItem("savedSearches"),
		max_saved_searches = 5;

	$(document).ready(function () {

		function submitKeywordSearch() {


			if ($("#q").val() && $("#q").val().length > 2 || exceptionKeywordsArray.indexOf($("#q").val()) != -1) {


				if ( !savedSearches ) savedSearches = [];

				var arrPos = $.inArray( '' + $('#q').val() , savedSearches);

				switch (arrPos) {

					case -1:

						if ( savedSearches.unshift(	'' + $('#q').val() ) > max_saved_searches ) {

							savedSearches.pop();

						}

						break;

					case 0:

						break;

					default:

						savedSearches.unshift( savedSearches.splice( arrPos, 1 )[0] );

				}

				localStorage.setItem( 'savedSearches', JSON.stringify(savedSearches) );



				if( $('#KeywordSearchUrl').length ) {


					document.location.href = $('#KeywordSearchUrl').val() + encodeURIComponent($("#q").val());



				} else {


					$("#keyword").val( encodeURIComponent($("#q").val()));
					$("#submenuSearch").submit();

				}

			}

			return false;

		}

		$("#submenuSearch button").on("click", function () {


			submitKeywordSearch();

        });

		$("#q").keyup( function(event) {

			if (event.keyCode == 13) {


				submitKeywordSearch();

			}

		});



		if ( savedSearches ) {

			$('#submenuSearch fieldset').append(
				'<div class="recentSearches">' +
					'<b>Your recent searches</b>' +
					'<ul></ul>' +
				'</div>'
			);

			savedSearches = JSON.parse(savedSearches);

			for ( i=0 ; i<savedSearches.length; i++ ) {

				$('#submenuSearch ul').append(

					'<li>' + savedSearches[i] + '</li>'

				);

			}

			$('#submenuSearch li').click( function (){

				$('#q').val($(this).html());
	            $("#submenuSearch button").click();

			});

		}

	});
          </script>
          <script>
           /* /js/components/start-form */

    $(document).ready(function () {
        /* /js/components/component-product-search-form.js */
        var productSearchView = {
            "DropdownLists": $('#finder .options'),
            "WhatDropDownFilter": $('.tagFilters .options label'),
            "WhereDropDownFilter": $('.geoFilters .options label'),
            "WhenDropDownFilter": $('.whenFilters .options label'),
            "WhereDropdownList": $('#finder .geoFilters .options'),
            "SearchButton": $('#finder button'),
            "Initialization": function () {

                // Search button OnClik Event
                productSearchView.SearchButton.on('click', function (e) {

                    var requestDataParameter = {
                        "SearchSettings": GetAjaxSearchSettingsModel( window["holidayFinderViewModel"]),
                        "Pager": null,
                    };


                    var url = window["holidayFinderViewModel"].HolidayFinderPageLink;

                    post(url, { "data": JSON.stringify(requestDataParameter) });



                    function post(path, params, method) {
                        method = method || "post"; // Set method to post by default if not specified.

                        // The rest of this code assumes you are not using a library.
                        // It can be made less wordy if you use one.
                        var form = document.createElement("form");
                        form.setAttribute("method", method);
                        form.setAttribute("action", path);

                        for (var key in params) {
                            if (params.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                                var hiddenField = document.createElement("input");
                                hiddenField.setAttribute("type", "hidden");
                                hiddenField.setAttribute("name", key);
                                hiddenField.setAttribute("value", params[key]);

                                form.appendChild(hiddenField);
                            }
                        }

                        document.body.appendChild(form);
                        form.submit();
                    }

                    return false;
                });

$('#finder .select:not(.disabled)').on('click', function (e) {

                    $(this).toggleClass('open');

                    /* 7.12.15 iulia - automatically scroll down to view all the options */
                    var optH = $("#finder").offset().top;
                    $('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: (optH - 200) }, 'fast');

                });
                //Dropdown lists
                productSearchView.DropdownLists.on('click', 'input', function (e) {

                    var that = $(this);
                    var searchSettings = window["holidayFinderViewModel"];
                    var dropdawnBox = $(that.parents('.select')[0]);

                    that
                        .parents('.select')
                        .toggleClass('open')
                        .find('.display span').html(that.next().html());

                    that
                        .parent().addClass('selected')
                        .siblings().removeClass('selected');

                    if (dropdawnBox.hasClass("tagFilters")) {

                        searchSettings.WhatFilter = null;
                        searchSettings.IsWhatFilterSelected = false;

                        $.each(searchSettings.WhatFiltersOptions, function (index, filter) {

                            if (filter["Id"] == that.val()) {
                                console.log(filter);

                                if (!searchSettings.WhatFilter) {
                                    searchSettings.WhatFilter = [];
                                }

                                searchSettings.WhatFilter.push(filter);
                                searchSettings.IsWhatFilterSelected = true;
                            }
                        });
                    }

                    if (dropdawnBox.hasClass("geoFilters")) {

                        searchSettings.WhereFilter = null;
                        searchSettings.IsWhereFilterSelected = false;

                        $.each(searchSettings.WhereFiltersOptions, function (index, filter) {

                            if (filter["Id"] == that.val()) {
                                console.log(filter);

                                searchSettings.WhereFilter = filter;

                                searchSettings.IsWhereFilterSelected = true;
                            }
                        });
                    }

                    if (dropdawnBox.hasClass("whenFilters")) {
                        searchSettings.WhenFilter = null;
                        searchSettings.IsWhenFilterSelected = false;
                        $.each(searchSettings.WhenFiltersOptions, function (index, filter) {


                            if (filter["Id"] == that.val()) {
                                console.log(filter);

                                if (!searchSettings.WhenFilter) {
                                    searchSettings.WhenFilter = [];
                                }
                                searchSettings.WhenFilter.push(filter);

                                searchSettings.IsWhenFilterSelected = true;
                            }
                        });
                    }

                });
            }
        };

        productSearchView.Initialization();
    });
          </script>
          <script>
           function GetAjaxSearchSettingsModel(searchSettings)
                    {
                        var newObject = $.extend(true, {}, searchSettings);

                        delete  newObject.WhatFiltersOptions ;
                        delete   newObject.WhereFiltersOptions;
                        delete   newObject.WhenFiltersOptions;

                        return newObject;
                    }
          </script>

           $(document).ready(function(){

		var t = $("h1").eq(0).text();
		var art = ($(".posts article").length > 1) ? 1 : 0;
		$(".blog-cat article, .blog-tag article").eq(art).attr("data-title", t).addClass("special");

			08.03.2016 - iulia - if less the 4 in a row than expand the images on that row. Issue: images are stretched.

			var neww = 100/(p - 4);

			}
			*/
		}

	});

	function getPosts(elem){
		var url = $(elem).attr("data-url");

		//show loading
		$(".navigation").remove();
		$(".posts").last().css("padding-bottom", "150px");
		loading("", $(".posts:last-of-type"), "", ($(".posts:last-of-type").height() / 2 + 50)); //471

		$.ajax({
			url: url,
			success: function (data) {
				closeLoading();
				$(".posts").last().css("padding-bottom", "0");

				if (data) {
					$(".posts").last().after(data);
				}

			}
		});
	}

        </nav>
       </li>
      </div>
     </nav>
    </li>
